2552  function gettrangaus(lowerLim,upperLim,avg,std) result(tranGaus)
2553 #if INTEL_COMPILER_ENABLED && defined DLL_ENABLED && (OS_IS_WINDOWS || defined OS_IS_DARWIN)
2554  !DEC$ ATTRIBUTES DLLEXPORT :: getTranGaus
2555 #endif
2556  ! getTranGaus Pseudorandom numbers from a truncated Gaussian distribution.
2557  !
2558  ! X = getTranGaus(lowerLim,B) returns a pseudorandom variable generated from a normal
2559  ! distribution with mean zero and standard deviation one (i.e. standard
2560  ! normal distribution) truncated to the interval [lowerLim,B].
2561  !
2562  ! X = getTranGaus(lowerLim,B,avg,std) returns a pseudorandom variable generated from
2563  ! a normal distribution with mean avg and standard deviation std
2564  ! truncated to the interval [lowerLim,B].
2565  !
2566  ! [X,P] = getTranGaus(...) also returns the vector of probabilities of X.
2567  !
2568  ! This implements an extension of the algorithm of Chopin detailed in
2569  ! N. Chopin, "Fast simulation of truncated Gaussian distributions", Stat
2570  ! Comput (2011) 21:275-288
2571  !
2572  ! Copyright (C) 2014 Vincent Mazet (ICube, CNRS/Université de Strasbourg),
2573  ! Version 2014-09-09, vincent.mazet@unistra.fr
2574  ! 18/06/2012:
2575  ! - first launch of getTranGaus.m
2576  ! 05/07/2012:
2577  ! - fix bug concerning the computing of the pdf when (avg,std) is
2578  ! different from (0,1).
2579  ! - fix bug about some indexes out of bounds when computing yl for some
2580  ! values of the input arguments.
2581  ! 04/09/2012:
2582  ! - change condition in line 2628 to fix a bug.
2583  ! 09/09/2014:
2584  ! - replace "variance" by "standard deviation" in the comments (thanks
2585  ! Umberto).
2586  !
2587  ! Licence: GNU Lesser General Public License Version 2
2588  ! This program is free software; you can redistribute it and/or modify it
2589  ! under the terms of the GNU Lesser General Public License as published by the
2590  ! Free Software Foundation; either version 2 of the License, or (at your
2591  ! option) any later version. This program is distributed in the hope that
2592  ! it will be useful, but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied
2593  ! warranty of MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE. See the
2594  ! GNU Lesser General Public License for more details. You should have received a
2595  ! copy of the GNU Lesser General Public License along with this program; if not,
2596  ! see http://www.gnu.org/licenses/old-licenses/gpl-2.0.txt
2597 
2598  use constants_mod, only: ik, rk
2599  implicit none
2600  real(rk), intent(in) :: lowerlim,upperlim
2601  real(rk), intent(in), optional :: avg, std
2602  real(rk) :: trangaus !,p
2603  real(rk) :: lowerlimstd,upperlimstd, mean, stdev
2604 
2605  mean = 0._rk
2606  stdev = 1._rk
2607  if (present(avg)) mean = avg
2608  if (present(std)) stdev = std
2609 
2610  ! Scaling
2611  lowerlimstd = (lowerlim-avg)/stdev
2612  upperlimstd = (upperlim-avg)/stdev
2613  trangaus = getstdtrangaus(lowerlimstd,upperlimstd) ! Generate the random variables
2614 
2615  ! Scaling
2616  trangaus = trangaus * stdev + avg
2617 
2618  !! Compute the probabilities
2619  !if (present(p)) then
2620  ! Z = sqrt(pi/2)*std * (erf(upperLim/sqrt(2))-erf(lowerLim/sqrt(2)))
2621  ! Z = max(Z,1e-15) ! Avoid NaN
2622  ! p = exp(-(tranGaus-mu).^2/2/std**2) / Z
2623  !end if
2624 
2625  end function gettrangaus
2626 
2627 !%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
2628 
2640  recursive function getstdtrangaus(lowerLim,upperLim) result(stdTranGaus)
2641 #if INTEL_COMPILER_ENABLED && defined DLL_ENABLED && (OS_IS_WINDOWS || defined OS_IS_DARWIN)
2642  !DEC$ ATTRIBUTES DLLEXPORT :: getStdTranGaus
2643 #endif
2644 
2645  use constants_mod, only: ik, rk
2646  use statistics_mod, only: getrandint, getrandgaus
2647  use iso_fortran_env, only: output_unit
2648 
2649  implicit none
2650 
2651  real(rk), intent(in) :: lowerlim, upperlim
2652  real(rk) :: stdtrangaus
2653 
2654  real(rk), parameter :: xmin = -2.00443204036_rk
2655  real(rk), parameter :: xmax = +3.48672170399_rk
2656 
2657  ! Design variables
2658  !integer(IK), parameter :: LEN_VEC_YU = 4001 !< Index of the right tail
2659  integer(IK), parameter :: kmin = 5_ik
2660  integer(IK), parameter :: i0 = 3271_ik
2661  real(rk) :: invh = 1631.73284006_rk
2662  real(rk) :: alpha = 1.837877066409345_rk
2663  real(rk) :: yl0 = 0.053513975472_rk
2664  real(rk) :: yln = 0.000914116389555_rk
2665 
2666  real(rk) :: twicelowerlim, explowerupper, z, neglogunifrnd, unifrnd, unifrndfixed
2667  real(rk) :: sim, simy, ylk, d, lowerbound !, u
2668  integer(IK) :: i, ka, kb, k
2669 
2670  ! Check if lowerLim < upperLim
2671 
2672  blockrange: if (lowerlim>=upperlim) then
2673 
2674  ! LCOV_EXCL_START
2675  write(output_unit,"(A)") module_name//"@getStdTranGaus: upperLim must be greater than lowerLim."
2676  error stop
2677  ! LCOV_EXCL_STOP
2678 
2679  ! Check if |lowerLim| < |upperLim|
2680  elseif (abs(lowerlim)>abs(upperlim)) then blockrange
2681 
2682  stdtrangaus = -getstdtrangaus(-upperlim,-lowerlim)
2683 
2684  ! If lowerLim in the right tail (lowerLim > xmax), use rejection algorithm with a truncated exponential proposal
2685  elseif (lowerlim > xmax) then blockrange
2686 
2687  twicelowerlim = 2_rk * lowerlim**2;
2688  explowerupper = exp(-lowerlim*(upperlim-lowerlim)) - 1._rk;
2689  do
2690  call random_number(unifrnd)
2691  z = log(1 + unifrnd*explowerupper)
2692  call random_number(unifrnd)
2693  neglogunifrnd = -log(unifrnd)
2694  if (twicelowerlim*neglogunifrnd > z**2) exit
2695  end do
2696  stdtrangaus = lowerlim - z / lowerlim
2697 
2698  ! If lowerLim in the left tail (lowerLim < xmin), use rejection algorithm with a Gaussian proposal
2699  elseif (lowerlim<xmin) then blockrange
2700 
2701  do ! LCOV_EXCL_LINE
2702  stdtrangaus = getrandgaus();
2703  if ( (stdtrangaus>=lowerlim) .and. (stdtrangaus<=upperlim) ) exit
2704  end do
2705 
2706  ! In other cases (xmin < lowerLim < xmax), use the algorithm of Chopin
2707  else blockrange
2708 
2709  ! Large data tables and design variables are used here
2710 
2711  ! Compute ka and kb
2712  i = i0 + floor(lowerlim*invh)
2713  ka = vec_cell(i+1) ! +1 due to index offset in Fortran
2714  if (upperlim >= xmax) then
2715  kb = len_vec_yu
2716  else
2717  i = i0 + floor(upperlim*invh)
2718  kb = vec_cell(i+1) ! +1 due to index offset in Fortran
2719  end if
2720 
2721  ! If |upperLim-lowerLim| is small, use rejection algorithm with a truncated exponential proposal
2722  if (abs(kb-ka) < kmin) then
2723  twicelowerlim = 2._rk*lowerlim**2
2724  explowerupper = exp(-lowerlim*(upperlim-lowerlim)) - 1._rk
2725  do
2726  call random_number(unifrnd)
2727  z = log( 1._rk + unifrnd*explowerupper )
2728  call random_number(unifrnd)
2729  neglogunifrnd = -log(unifrnd);
2730  if (twicelowerlim*neglogunifrnd > z**2) exit
2731  end do
2732  stdtrangaus = lowerlim - z/lowerlim
2733  return
2734  end if
2735 
2736  do ! LCOV_EXCL_LINE
2737 
2738  ! Sample integer between ka and kb
2739  k = getrandint(ka,kb) + 1_ik; ! +1 due to index offset in Fortran
2740 
2741  if (k == len_vec_yu + 1_ik) then
2742 
2743  ! Right tail
2744 
2745  lowerbound = vec_x(len_vec_x);
2746  call random_number(unifrnd)
2747  z = -log(unifrnd);
2748  call random_number(unifrnd)
2749  neglogunifrnd = -log(unifrnd);
2750  z = z / lowerbound;
2751  if ( (z**2 <= 2._rk*neglogunifrnd) .and. (z < upperlim-lowerbound) ) then
2752  ! Accept this proposition, otherwise reject
2753  stdtrangaus = lowerbound + z
2754  return
2755  end if
2756 
2757  elseif ( (k<=ka+2) .or. (k>=kb .and. upperlim<xmax) ) then
2758 
2759  ! Two leftmost and rightmost regions
2760 
2761  call random_number(unifrnd)
2762  sim = vec_x(k) + (vec_x(k+1_ik)-vec_x(k)) * unifrnd;
2763  if ( (sim >= lowerlim) .and. (sim <= upperlim) ) then
2764 
2765  ! Accept this proposition, otherwise reject
2766  call random_number(unifrnd)
2767  simy = vec_yu(k)*unifrnd
2768 
2769  ! Compute y_l from y_k
2770  if (k == 1_ik) then
2771  ylk = yl0
2772  elseif (k == len_vec_yu) then
2773  ylk = yln
2774  elseif (k <= 1954_ik) then
2775  ylk = vec_yu(k-1_ik)
2776  else
2777  ylk = vec_yu(k+1_ik)
2778  end if
2779 
2780  if ( (simy<ylk) .or. (sim**2 + 2._rk*log(simy) + alpha < 0._rk) ) then
2781  stdtrangaus = sim
2782  return
2783  end if
2784 
2785  end if
2786 
2787  else
2788 
2789  ! All the other boxes
2790 
2791  call random_number(unifrndfixed)
2792  simy = vec_yu(k) * unifrndfixed;
2793  d = vec_x(k+1_ik) - vec_x(k);
2794 
2795  ! Compute y_l from y_k
2796  if (k == 1_ik) then
2797  ylk = yl0
2798  elseif (k == len_vec_yu) then
2799  ylk = yln
2800  elseif (k <= 1954_ik) then
2801  ylk = vec_yu(k-1_ik)
2802  else
2803  ylk = vec_yu(k+1_ik)
2804  end if
2805 
2806  if (simy < ylk) then ! That is what happens most of the time
2807  stdtrangaus = vec_x(k) + unifrndfixed*d*vec_yu(k) / ylk
2808  return
2809  end if
2810  call random_number(unifrnd)
2811  sim = vec_x(k) + d * unifrnd
2812  ! Otherwise, check if we are below the pdf curve
2813  if (sim**2 + 2*log(simy) + alpha < 0) then
2814  stdtrangaus = sim
2815  return
2816  end if
2817 
2818  end if
2819 
2820  end do
2821 
2822  end if blockrange
2823 
2824  end function getstdtrangaus
2825
